<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user, an architect, requires a comprehensive internal project management application for their firm, 4th Dimension.

**PRODUCT REQUIREMENTS (Evolved):**
1.  **User Management & Dashboards:**
    *   Role-based access with an Owner Dashboard for project and team oversight.
    *   A system for inviting, approving, and assigning specific roles (e.g., Senior Architect, 3D Visualizer) to users.
2.  **Project & Drawing Workflow:**
    *   A comment-based revision system.
    *   Automatic creation of default drawing lists for new projects.
3.  **Accounting (Owner-Only):**
    *   A system to track project fees, income, and expenses.
    *   A simple dashboard for clients to view their fee status.
4.  **Social Media Management:**
    *   An automated system to create and schedule social media posts.
5.  **Notifications:**
    *   A robust, real-time, multi-channel (In-App, Email, WhatsApp) notification system for 12 key application events, with different message templates for different audiences (client, team).

**User's preferred language**: English

**what currently exists?**
The application is a full-stack React/FastAPI/MongoDB solution. This session focused heavily on implementing a brand-new notification system based on user specifications and fixing a series of related bugs. Key accomplishments include:
*   **New Notification System:** A complete backend implementation with separate services for sending notifications () and triggering them ().
*   **Critical UI Fix:** Resolved a major bug that caused the frontend to hang and become unresponsive when the notification bell was clicked. This was fixed by replacing the problematic component with a new stable one ().
*   **Enhanced User Management:** The user approval process now includes a dropdown with a full list of roles. The workflow for rejected users was fixed, allowing them to re-register without being blocked.
*   **Simplified Invites:** The Invite Member feature was streamlined to only require a name and phone number, sending a direct WhatsApp invitation.
*   **Login & Data Integrity:** Fixed a critical login failure by recreating the owner's account and corrected dashboard data by filtering out non-approved users.

**Last working item**:
-   Last item agent was working: The user reported that the automated welcome emails sent to newly approved team members are plain text and curt, not the beautiful HTML templates that were previously used. The agent was tasked with restoring the original, professionally formatted HTML emails.
-   Status: **NOT STARTED**
-   Agent Testing Done: N

Update the  function in  to handle HTML content. 3. Trigger a user approval to send a test email. 4. Ask the user to confirm receipt and formatting of the new email.
-   User Testing Done: N
